### üë§ **User** *(07.12.2025, 16:03)*

# Dialog Web UI

Launch the web interface for browsing and managing Claude Code dialogs.

## Command

```bash
npm run dialog:ui
```

Or directly:
```bash
node .claude-export/dist/cli.js ui
```

## Features

- Browse all exported dialogs
- Toggle visibility (public/private)
- Search across dialogs
- View dialog details
- Manage .gitignore entries

## Usage

1. Run the command above
2. Open http://localhost:3333 in browser
3. Browse and manage your dialogs
4. Press Ctrl+C to stop

## Options

```bash
npm run dialog:ui -- --port 8080  # Custom port
```

## Notes

- Dialogs are private by default (in .gitignore)
- Toggle visibility to share specific dialogs
- All processing is local, no external APIs

```json

```

```
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ claude-export/
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ cli.js, server.js, etc.
‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ public/          ‚Üê Teacher UI

‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ html-viewer/         ‚Üê Student UI template
```

Summary:
## 1. Primary Request and Intent

The user's primary requests evolved through the conversation:
1. **Initial Request**: Understand the project (Claude Code Starter v2.0 framework)
2. **Main Task**: Fix and test the dialog export UI system after merging code from `/Users/alexeykrolmini/Downloads/Code/claude-export` into `Project_init`
3. **Specific Goals**:
   - Get Teacher UI working (localhost:3333)
   - Get Student UI working (html-viewer/index.html)
   - Ensure both UIs work independently
   - Test with public dialogs to verify Student UI displays content

## 2. Key Technical Concepts

- **Claude Code Starter Framework**: Meta-documentation framework for AI-assisted development with modular architecture
- **Two Independent UIs**:
  - **Teacher UI**: TypeScript SPA (Express server on port 3333) for managing dialog visibility
  - **Student UI**: Static HTML viewer (standalone file) for read-only access to public dialogs
- **Watcher vs UI Separation**: Watcher monitors JSONL sessions for auto-export; UI only reads exported MD files
- **Build Process**: TypeScript compilation + asset copying (public/, html-viewer/)
- **Template Replacement**: Static HTML generation using placeholder replacement (`__DIALOGS_DATA__`, `__PROJECT_INFO__`, etc.)
- **Privacy by Default**: New dialogs added to .gitignore, can be toggled public via Teacher UI

- **Cause**: server.ts was initializing SessionWatcher on startup, which called `process.exit(1)` when no active JSONL sessions found
- **User Feedback**: "UI –≤–æ–æ–±—â–µ –Ω–µ –¥–æ–ª–∂–µ–Ω –∏—Å–∫–∞—Ç—å —Ç–≤–æ–∏ —Å–µ—Å—Å–∏–∏, –æ–Ω –¥–æ–ª–∂–µ–Ω —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞—Ç—å —Å —ç–∫—Å–ø—Ä—Ç–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–º–∏" - UI should only work with exported MD files, not JSONL
- **Fix**: Removed watcher initialization from server.ts entirely (lines 34, 37, 458-459, 492-494)

- **Cause**: Static files (public/) weren't being copied to dist/ during build

- **Fix**: 
  1. Updated build script to copy public/ to dist/claude-export/

- **User Feedback**: Explained this is Student UI, not temporary files
- **Fix**:

- Debug output shows replacements working: "Template length before: 20557, Template length after: 676064"
- But the actual file on disk shows: 788 lines (same size as template)

**Current hypothesis**: There's a discrepancy between what's being logged and what's being written to disk. Possible causes:
- File write is failing silently after logging
- Wrong file path being written vs read
- Browser caching old version
- Output is being written somewhere else

### ü§ñ **Claude** *(07.12.2025, 16:54)*

## Bug Fixed!

**Root Cause**: The dialog content from a previous session mentioned the placeholder strings `__PROJECT_INFO__` and `__DIALOGS_DATA__` in conversation. When we replaced `__DIALOGS_DATA__` first, it embedded JSON content containing these strings. Then `template.replace('__PROJECT_INFO__', ...)` found the string in the embedded content first (not the actual placeholder), replacing the wrong occurrence.

**Solution**: Changed replacement order in `exporter.ts:835-844`:
- Replace simple placeholders (PROJECT_INFO, VERSION, DATE, etc.) **first**  
- Replace DIALOGS_DATA **last** (after all other placeholders are replaced)

This ensures actual template placeholders are replaced before dialog content is embedded.

The Student UI (html-viewer/index.html) should now display all 7 public dialogs correctly. The file has been opened in your browser.

---

5. **–ì–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—è summary** –¥–ª—è –¥–∏–∞–ª–æ–≥–æ–≤

–í—ã —Ö–æ—Ç–∏—Ç–µ, —á—Ç–æ–±—ã —è —Å–æ—Å—Ä–µ–¥–æ—Ç–æ—á–∏–ª—Å—è –Ω–∞ —á–µ–º-—Ç–æ –∫–æ–Ω–∫—Ä–µ—Ç–Ω–æ–º?

   - –î–ª—è –∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω–æ–π —Å–µ—Å—Å–∏–∏ - –ø—Ä–æ–º–µ–∂—É—Ç–æ—á–Ω–æ–µ summary

   - **–ü—Ä–∞–≤–∞ –¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–∞** - –Ω–µ –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –ø—Ä–æ—á–∏—Ç–∞—Ç—å `~/.config/claude/sessions/`
   - **–õ–æ–≥–∏–∫–∞ –æ–ø—Ä–µ–¥–µ–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è "–∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω–æ–π"** - –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –±—ã—Ç—å –±–∞–≥ –≤ –∫–æ–¥–µ, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–π —Ä–µ—à–∞–µ—Ç, —á—Ç–æ –∞–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω–∞—è —Å–µ—Å—Å–∏—è = "–∑–∞–∫—Ä—ã—Ç–∞—è" –∏–ª–∏ –Ω–∞–æ–±–æ—Ä–æ—Ç
   - **–ú—ã —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–µ–º –∏–∑ –¥—Ä—É–≥–æ–≥–æ –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—è/–ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç–∞** - –Ω–µ—Å–æ–æ—Ç–≤–µ—Ç—Å—Ç–≤–∏–µ –ø—É—Ç–µ–π

## –ß—Ç–æ –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏—Ç—å:

–ù—É–∂–Ω–æ –ø–æ—Å–º–æ—Ç—Ä–µ—Ç—å –∫–æ–¥ –∫–Ω–æ–ø–∫–∏ Force Sync –∏ –ª–æ–≥–∏–∫—É –ø–æ–∏—Å–∫–∞ —Å–µ—Å—Å–∏–π. –ü–æ–∫–∞–∑–∞—Ç—å?

### –ö–∞–∫ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–µ—Ç Student UI?

**–ß—Ç–æ –ø—Ä–æ–∏—Å—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç:**
```typescript
// exporter.ts:810-850
function generateStaticHtml(projectPath: string) {
  // 1. –ß–∏—Ç–∞–µ—Ç template.html
  let template = fs.readFileSync('html-viewer/template.html');
  
  // 2. –°–æ–±–∏—Ä–∞–µ—Ç –≤—Å–µ –ü–£–ë–õ–ò–ß–ù–´–ï –¥–∏–∞–ª–æ–≥–∏
  const dialogs = getExportedDialogs(projectPath)
    .filter(d => d.isPublic);
  
  // 3. –ó–∞–º–µ–Ω—è–µ—Ç placeholders:
  template = template.replace('__PROJECT_INFO__', JSON.stringify(projectInfo));
  template = template.replace('__DIALOGS_DATA__', JSON.stringify(dialogs));
  
  // 4. –ü–∏—à–µ—Ç –≤ html-viewer/index.html
  fs.writeFileSync('html-viewer/index.html', template);
}
```

**2. –ß—Ç–æ –≤—Å—Ç—Ä–∞–∏–≤–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –≤ HTML:**

```html
    content: "<!-- –ø–æ–ª–Ω—ã–π markdown –¥–∏–∞–ª–æ–≥–∞ -->",
    summary: "...",
    ...
  },
  // ... –≤—Å–µ –ø—É–±–ª–∏—á–Ω—ã–µ –¥–∏–∞–ª–æ–≥–∏
];

  name: "Project_init",
  path: "/Users/.../Project_init",
```

### –ü—Ä–µ–∏–º—É—â–µ—Å—Ç–≤–∞:

‚úÖ **–ê–≤—Ç–æ–Ω–æ–º–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å** ‚Äî –Ω–µ —Ç—Ä–µ–±—É–µ—Ç —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä–∞

‚úÖ **–£–¥–æ–±—Å—Ç–≤–æ** ‚Äî –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ —Ä–∞–∑–º–µ—Å—Ç–∏—Ç—å –Ω–∞ GitHub Pages  
‚úÖ **–ü—Ä–æ–∏–∑–≤–æ–¥–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å** ‚Äî –≤—Å–µ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ —É–∂–µ –≤ –±—Ä–∞—É–∑–µ—Ä–µ

### ‚úÖ –ß—Ç–æ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–µ—Ç –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏–ª—å–Ω–æ:

**1. –ü–æ—Å–ª–µ–¥–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å –≤ `npm run dialog:export`:**
```typescript
// cli.ts:131-150

  // –®–ê–ì 1: –≠–∫—Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç markdown (–≤–∫–ª—é—á–∞—è —Ç–µ–∫—É—â—É—é —Å–µ—Å—Å–∏—é)
```

**2. –ü—É—Ç–∏ –¥–ª—è HTML –≥–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–∏:**
```typescript
// exporter.ts:756-770
function getTemplatePath() {
  // –ß–∏—Ç–∞–µ—Ç: dist/html-viewer/template.html ‚úÖ
  return path.join(__dirname, '..', 'html-viewer', 'template.html');

// exporter.ts:778-785
function generateStaticHtml(targetProjectPath) {
  const viewerFolder = path.join(targetProjectPath, 'html-viewer');
  const outputPath = path.join(viewerFolder, 'index.html');
  // –ü–∏—à–µ—Ç: {project}/html-viewer/index.html ‚úÖ
}
```

**3. –î–∏—Ä–µ–∫—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∏:**
| –§–∞–π–ª | –ü—É—Ç—å | –ù–∞–∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ |
|------|------|------------|
| **Template (source)** | `html-viewer/template.html` | –í Git, –∏—Å—Ö–æ–¥–Ω–∏–∫ |
| **Template (dist)** | `dist/html-viewer/template.html` | –ö–æ–ø–∏—è –ø—Ä–∏ build, —á–∏—Ç–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –∫–æ–¥–æ–º |
| **Output** | `html-viewer/index.html` | –í Git, –¥–ª—è —Å—Ç—É–¥–µ–Ω—Ç–æ–≤ |

### ‚ö†Ô∏è –ù–µ–±–æ–ª—å—à–∞—è –Ω–µ–æ–ø—Ç–∏–º–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å:


–ö–æ–ø–∏—Ä—É–µ—Ç **–≤–µ—Å—å** `html-viewer/` –≤–∫–ª—é—á–∞—è —Å—Ç–∞—Ä—ã–π `index.html` ‚Üí `dist/html-viewer/index.html`

**–ù–æ —ç—Ç–æ –Ω–µ –∫—Ä–∏—Ç–∏—á–Ω–æ!** –§–∞–π–ª `dist/html-viewer/index.html` –Ω–∏–∫–æ–≥–¥–∞ –Ω–µ –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É–µ—Ç—Å—è:
- –ö–æ–¥ —á–∏—Ç–∞–µ—Ç —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ `dist/html-viewer/template.html` ‚úÖ

## 2. Key Technical Concepts

- **Two Independent UIs:**
  - **Teacher UI**: TypeScript SPA on Express server (localhost:3333), manages dialog visibility
  - **Student UI**: Static HTML file, self-contained, read-only for public dialogs
- **Template Replacement**: Placeholders (`__PROJECT_INFO__`, `__DIALOGS_DATA__`) replaced with JSON data
- **Sprint Completion Protocol**: build ‚Üí update metafiles ‚Üí export ‚Üí commit ‚Üí push
- **Privacy by Default**: New dialogs added to .gitignore, toggled public via Teacher UI
- **Static HTML Generation**: Embeds all public dialog data into single HTML file for distribution

## 3. Files and Code Sections

### `/Users/alexeykrolmini/Downloads/Code/Project_init/src/claude-export/exporter.ts`

**Why Important:** Core logic for generating Student UI static HTML

**Changes Made (lines 753-766):**
```typescript
/**
 * Get template path for static HTML viewer
 * Always reads from project root html-viewer/template.html
 */
function getTemplatePath(): string {
  // Template is always in project root (not in dist/)
  const templatePath = path.join(process.cwd(), 'html-viewer', 'template.html');

  if (!fs.existsSync(templatePath)) {
    throw new Error('Template not found. Make sure html-viewer/template.html exists in project root.');
  }

  return templatePath;
}
```

**Replacement Order (lines 835-856):**
```typescript
// Replace simple placeholders first, before embedding dialog content
// (dialog content may mention these placeholders in conversation)
template = template.replace('__PROJECT_INFO__', JSON.stringify(projectInfo));
template = template.replace('__VERSION__', 'v2.3.0');
template = template.replace('__DATE__', dateStr);
template = template.replace('__DATETIME__', dateTimeStr);
template = template.replace('__PROJECT_NAME__', projectName);

// Replace dialog data last (may contain placeholder strings in content)
template = template.replace('__DIALOGS_DATA__', JSON.stringify(dialogsData));

// Write output
fs.writeFileSync(outputPath, template);
```

## 4. Errors and Fixes

### Error 1: Student UI Template Replacement Order
**Description:** DIALOGS_DATA was replaced first, embedding placeholder strings from dialog content. Then PROJECT_INFO replacement found the placeholder string INSIDE the embedded JSON, not the actual template placeholder.

**Fix:** Changed replacement order in exporter.ts - replace simple placeholders (PROJECT_INFO, VERSION, etc.) BEFORE replacing DIALOGS_DATA.

**User Feedback:** User identified the issue was related to embedded content containing placeholder strings.

### Error 2: Path Encoding Mismatch
**Description:** Project directory name `Project_init` (underscore) but Claude sessions directory was `Project-init` (dash). `findClaudeProjectDir()` couldn't match them.

**Fix:** Added variation support in exporter.ts:175-185:
```typescript
// Try with underscore ‚Üí dash conversion (Claude may convert underscores)
const withDashes = normalized.replace(/_/g, '-');
if (withDashes !== normalized && fs.existsSync(path.join(PROJECTS_DIR, withDashes))) {
  return withDashes;
}
```

**User Feedback:** User confirmed this was a critical bug affecting Force Sync and all session discovery.

### Error 3: Legacy File Duplication
**Description:** Both `html-viewer/index.html` (1MB, current) and `dist/html-viewer/index.html` (870KB, outdated) existed.

**Fix:** 
1. Deleted `dist/html-viewer/` entirely
2. Modified `getTemplatePath()` to only read from project root
3. Removed html-viewer copying from build script

**User Feedback:** "–í—Å–µ –ª–∏—à–Ω–∏–µ —Ñ–∞–π–ª—ã —É–¥–∞–ª–∏—Ç—å... –¥–æ–ª–∂–Ω—ã –±—ã—Ç—å —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –≤ /Users/alexeykrolmini/Downloads/Code/Project_init/html-viewer"

### ü§ñ **Claude** *(07.12.2025, 18:01)*

**Found the bug!** JSON parse error - the dialog content has **unterminated strings**. This means the dialog content isn't being properly escaped when embedded into JSON.

Let me check how the exporter is generating the JSON for the static HTML:

---

### ü§ñ **Claude** *(07.12.2025, 18:02)*

The code uses `JSON.stringify()` which should escape properly. But the template has this:

```javascript
const DIALOGS_DATA = __DIALOGS_DATA__;
```

When we replace `__DIALOGS_DATA__` with `JSON.stringify(dialogsData)`, we get:

```javascript
const DIALOGS_DATA = [{"filename":"..."}];
```

This should work. Let me check if there's a character limit or special characters causing issues. Let me look at position ~95280 in the HTML:

---

### ü§ñ **Claude** *(07.12.2025, 18:02)*

I see the problem! There's TypeScript code with backticks (` ``` `) in the dialog content. When `JSON.stringify()` embeds this inside the `<script>` tag, it might not handle all edge cases for HTML context.

Let me check the actual structure to see if the JSON is closed properly:

---

### ü§ñ **Claude** *(07.12.2025, 18:02)*

Good! I can see the declarations are properly closed. But there's a JSON parse error at position 95280. The issue is that the dialog content contains characters that break the JSON when embedded in a `<script>` tag.

Let me check if the problem is the `</script>` sequence in the content which would break out of the script tag:

---

### ü§ñ **Claude** *(07.12.2025, 18:02)*

**Found it!** There are multiple `</script>` sequences in the embedded dialog content. When the browser parses the HTML, it sees `</script>` inside the JavaScript string and **closes the script tag prematurely**, breaking the JavaScript.

This is a classic HTML injection issue. The fix is to escape `</script>` in the JSON data. Let me update the exporter to handle this:

---

### ü§ñ **Claude** *(07.12.2025, 18:02)*

Perfect! Now let me rebuild and regenerate the Student UI to test the fix:

---

### ü§ñ **Claude** *(07.12.2025, 18:03)*

Good! Now let's verify the fix works - checking if the JSON can be parsed:

---

### ü§ñ **Claude** *(07.12.2025, 18:03)*

Still failing. The regex I'm using to extract the data is wrong - it stops at the first `];` which might be inside the JSON. Let me extract the data properly by finding the full JavaScript statement:

---

### ü§ñ **Claude** *(07.12.2025, 18:03)*

Excellent! The JSON **is valid** when extracted properly - 14 dialogs, 7 public. So the JSON structure is correct.

The problem must be how the browser parses the HTML. Let me check if the `</script>` escaping was applied:

---

### –¢–µ–∫—É—â–µ–µ —Å–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–∏–µ:

Analysis:
Let me chronologically analyze this conversation about fixing the Student UI in the Claude Code Starter framework.

## Initial Context:
The conversation began with a continuation from a previous session about the Claude Code Starter framework v2.0. The framework has two UIs:
1. Teacher UI (TypeScript SPA on localhost:3333) - manages dialog visibility
2. Student UI (static HTML in html-viewer/) - read-only for public dialogs

## Main Problem Discovery:
User showed a screenshot where Student UI was displaying "Loading..." despite having data embedded. This was the core issue to solve.

## Key Events:

1. **Script Tag Breaking Issue**: I discovered the JSON data contained `</script>` sequences that were breaking out of the script tag, causing browser parsing errors.
   - Fixed by escaping in exporter.ts:853: `.replace(/<\/script>/gi, '<\\/script>')`

2. **Private Dialogs in Student UI**: Found that Student UI was showing ALL 14 dialogs (public + private) instead of only public ones.
   - Fixed by adding filter in exporter.ts:824-825: `const publicDialogs = dialogsData.filter(d => d.isPublic);`
   - Updated embedding to use `publicDialogs` instead of `dialogsData`

3. **Synchronization Issue**: User made all dialogs public in Teacher UI and asked how to sync with Student UI.
   - Ran `npm run dialog:export` which regenerated Student UI
   - Discovered 6 new JSONL sessions that were exported (from Nov 9, Nov 23, Dec 7)

4. **November Sessions Question**: User asked why November sessions appeared.
   - Explained that Claude Code stores all sessions for a project in one directory
   - Sessions from Nov 9 and Nov 23 were legitimate old work on the Project_init framework

5. **Missing Summaries Issue**: User asked why some sessions lack summaries.
   - Found 3 files without summary: 2025-12-05_session-c57618da.md, 2025-12-06_session-a1fda585.md, 2025-12-07_session-4ad06f83.md
   - Discovered watcher.ts has automatic summary generation via Claude Haiku
   - User corrected me: "I should NOT manually run watcher" - everything must be AUTOMATIC in completion protocol

6. **Current Work - Making Summary Generation Automatic**:
   - User insisted: watcher has nothing to do with UI, it should automatically find desync, export, and create summaries during completion protocol
   - User: "Nothing should be manual. User should not finish anything manually."
   - Started modifying cli.ts to add automatic summary generation to `npm run dialog:export`
   - Exported `requestSummary` from watcher.ts
   - Added import in cli.ts
   - Modified `runExport` function to call `requestSummary` for all dialogs without summaries (except current session)

## Technical Details:

**Summary Format:**
```markdown
<!-- SUMMARY_SHORT: short description -->
<!-- SUMMARY_FULL: detailed description -->
```

**Summary Generation Process:**
- watcher.ts:47 `requestSummary()` spawns `claude --model haiku` with prompts
- For final summaries: detailed 3-5 sentence format
- For interim: 2-3 sentence format
- Automatically edits markdown files to add summary comments

**Current Implementation Status:**
- ‚úÖ Exported requestSummary from watcher.ts
- ‚úÖ Added import to cli.ts

Summary:
## 1. Primary Request and Intent

**Main Request:** Fix Student UI (static HTML viewer) that was showing "Loading..." despite having embedded data, then make the entire export process fully automatic.

**Sub-requests:**
1. Fix Student UI not displaying dialogs
2. Understand and explain why November dialogs appeared in exports
3. Understand why some sessions lack summaries

## 2. Key Technical Concepts

- **Two Independent UIs:**
  - Teacher UI: TypeScript SPA (localhost:3333), manages visibility, full access
  - Student UI: Static HTML (html-viewer/index.html), read-only, only public dialogs
- **HTML Script Tag Injection:** `</script>` in JSON data breaks browser parsing
- **Privacy by Default:** New dialogs added to .gitignore automatically
- **Summary Format:** HTML comments at start of markdown files
  - `<!-- SUMMARY_SHORT: ... -->` - one sentence for lists
  - `<!-- SUMMARY_FULL: ... -->` - 3-5 sentences with technical details
- **Claude Haiku Integration:** Automatic summary generation via CLI
- **Session Persistence:** Claude Code stores all project sessions in one directory regardless of date
- **Completion Protocol:** Automated workflow for finishing sprints

### `/Users/alexeykrolmini/Downloads/Code/Project_init/src/claude-export/cli.ts`

**Why Important:** Entry point for `npm run dialog:export` command - must handle automatic summary generation.

**Changes Made:**

**Line 15** - Added requestSummary import:
```typescript
import { startWatcher, requestSummary } from './watcher';
```

**Lines 144-162** - Added automatic summary generation in runExport:
```typescript
// Generate summaries for exported dialogs (except current session)
const dialogFiles = getDialogFiles(projectPath);
const currentSessionId = getCurrentSessionId(projectPath);

const dialogsWithoutSummary = dialogFiles.filter(filePath => {
  // Skip current session
  if (currentSessionId && filePath.includes(currentSessionId.substring(0, 8))) {
    return false;
  }
  // Check if has summary
  return !hasSummary(filePath);
});

if (dialogsWithoutSummary.length > 0) {
  console.log(`\nGenerating summaries for ${dialogsWithoutSummary.length} dialog(s)...`);
  for (const filePath of dialogsWithoutSummary) {
    requestSummary(filePath, false, true); // isFinal=true for completed sessions
  }
}
```

## 4. Errors and Fixes

### Error 1: Student UI Showing "Loading..."

**Description:** Browser showed "Loading..." message despite having 999KB of embedded data.

**Root Cause:** JSON parse error - dialog content contained literal `</script>` tags which prematurely closed the script tag in HTML, breaking JavaScript execution.

**Fix:** Added escaping in exporter.ts:853
```typescript
const dialogsDataJson = JSON.stringify(publicDialogs).replace(/<\/script>/gi, '<\\/script>');
```

**Verification:**
```bash
grep -o '</script>' html-viewer/index.html  # Only 1 result (the actual closing tag)
grep -o '<\\/script>' html-viewer/index.html  # 4 results (escaped in data)
```

**User Feedback:** None - fix worked immediately.

### Error 2: Private Dialogs Exposed in Student UI

**Description:** Student UI embedded ALL 14 dialogs (7 public + 7 private) instead of only public ones.

**Root Cause:** `generateStaticHtml()` in exporter.ts was embedding `dialogsData` (all dialogs) instead of filtering for `isPublic: true`.

**Fix:** Added filter before embedding (exporter.ts:824-825):
```typescript
const publicDialogs = dialogsData.filter(d => d.isPublic);
```

Then changed embedding to use `publicDialogs` instead of `dialogsData`.

**Verification:**
```bash
grep -o '"isPublic":true' html-viewer/index.html | wc -l   # 7
grep -o '"isPublic":false' html-viewer/index.html | wc -l  # 0
```

**User Feedback:** User confirmed this was correct after synchronization.

### Error 3: Stale Student UI Data

**Description:** Teacher UI and Student UI showed different dialog counts (15 vs 14).

**Root Cause:** Student UI html file was outdated. When regenerated, it triggered export of 6 previously unexported JSONL sessions from November and December.

**Fix:** Deleted old html file and ran `npm run dialog:export`, which:
1. Exported 6 new sessions to markdown
2. Added them to .gitignore (private by default)
3. Regenerated Student UI with current public dialogs

**User Feedback:** User questioned why November sessions appeared, which led to understanding that Claude Code stores all sessions for a project together regardless of date.

### Error 4: Missing Function Imports in cli.ts

**Description:** Added code calling `getDialogFiles`, `getCurrentSessionId`, `hasSummary` but didn't import them.

**Status:** **INCOMPLETE** - This is where work was interrupted. Still need to add these imports from appropriate modules.

## 5. Problem Solving

### Solved Problems:

1. **Student UI JavaScript Error**
   - Problem: Browser couldn't parse embedded JSON due to `</script>` in content
   - Solution: Escape regex replacement before embedding
   - Status: ‚úÖ Fixed and verified

2. **Privacy Leak in Student UI**
   - Problem: Private dialogs visible to students
   - Solution: Filter dialogs to only public before embedding
   - Status: ‚úÖ Fixed and verified

3. **Data Synchronization**
   - Problem: Teacher UI and Student UI out of sync
   - Solution: `npm run dialog:export` regenerates Student UI from current state
   - Status: ‚úÖ Working correctly

4. **November Sessions Mystery**
   - Problem: User confused about old session dates
   - Solution: Explained Claude Code's session storage architecture
   - Status: ‚úÖ Understood and accepted

### Ongoing Troubleshooting:

**Making Summary Generation Fully Automatic**
- Problem: Summary generation requires manual watcher invocation
- User Requirement: Must be 100% automatic during `npm run dialog:export`
- Current Status: Added code to call `requestSummary()` automatically but missing imports
- Remaining Work: Add missing imports and test the full flow

```typescript
const dialogsWithoutSummary = dialogFiles.filter(filePath => {
  // Skip current session
  if (currentSessionId && filePath.includes(currentSessionId.substring(0, 8))) {
    return false;
  }
  // Check if has summary
  return !hasSummary(filePath);  // ‚Üê –ì–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–∏—Ä—É–µ–º –¢–û–õ–¨–ö–û –µ—Å–ª–∏ hasSummary = false
});
```

**–í exporter.ts:619-627 (–∏—Å–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–Ω–∞—è —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü–∏—è hasSummary):**
```typescript
export function hasSummary(filePath: string): boolean {
  const content = fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf-8');
  return (
    SUMMARY_SHORT_PATTERN.test(content) ||    // –ù–æ–≤—ã–π —Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç SHORT
    SUMMARY_FULL_PATTERN.test(content) ||      // –ù–æ–≤—ã–π —Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç FULL
    SUMMARY_PATTERN.test(content) ||           // –°—Ç–∞—Ä—ã–π —Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç <!-- SUMMARY: -->
    SUMMARIES_SECTION_PATTERN.test(content)    // –°—Ç–∞—Ä—ã–π —Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç ## Summaries
  );
}
```
